All schema migrations (v0-v42) are executed in the backend\\n45: - Ports the logic from DashboardMigrator and implements built-in plugin migrations for panel plugins since backend cannot load plugins\\n46: - Transforms legacy JSON dashboards to migrated JSON format\\n47: - Handles backward compatibility for older dashboard formats\\n48: - See [SchemaVersion Migration Guide](./schemaversion/README.md) for detailed instructions on creating new schema migrations\\n49: \\n50: #### v1 to v2 Conversion:\\n51: - API version conversions between different Kubernetes API versions\\n52: - Transforms JSON dashboards to structured dashboard format\\n53: - v2 schema is the stable, typed schema with proper type definitions\\n54: - Handles modern dashboard features and Kubernetes-native storage\\n55: \\n56: ## Conversion Matrix\\n57: \\n58: The system supports conversions between all dashboard API versions:\\n59: \\n60: | From ↓ / To → | v0alpha1 | v1beta1 | v2alpha1 | v2beta1 |\\n61: |---------------|----------|---------|----------|---------|\\n62: | **v0alpha1**  | ✓        | ✓       | ✓        | ✓       |\\n63: | **v1beta1**   | ✓        | ✓       | ✓        | ✓       |\\n64: | **v2alpha1**  | ✓        | ✓       | ✓        | ✓       |\\n65: | **v2beta1**   | ✓        | ✓       | ✓        | ✓       |\\n66: \\n67: Each conversion path is automatically instrumented with metrics and logging.\\n68: \\n69: ## API Versions\\n70: \\n71: The supported dashboard API versions are:\\n72: \\n73: - `dashboard.grafana.app/v0alpha1` - Legacy JSON dashboard format\\n74: - `dashboard.grafana.app/v1beta1` - Migrated JSON dashboard format  \\n75: - `dashboard.grafana.app/v2alpha1` - New structured dashboard format\\n76: - `dashboard.grafana.app/v2beta1` - Enhanced structured dashboard format\\n77: \\n78: ## Schema Versions\\n79: \\n80: Schema versions (v13-v42) apply only to v0alpha1 and v1beta1 dashboards:\\n81: \\n82: - **Minimum supported version**: v13\\n83: - **Latest version**: v42  \\n84: - **Migration path**: Sequential (v13→v14→v15...→v42)\\n85: \\n86: For detailed information about creating schema version migrations, see the [SchemaVersion Migration Guide](./schemaversion/README.md).\\n87: \\n88: ## Testing\\n89: \\n90: The implementation includes comprehensive test coverage for conversion-level operations:\\n91: \\n92: - **Backend conversion tests**: API version conversions with metrics validation\\n93: - **Frontend tests**: TypeScript conversion tests  \\n94: - **Integration tests**: End-to-end conversion validation\\n95: -
